name:f‚Äçx‚Äçd‚Äç1‚Äç0‚Äç2‚Äç8
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:12 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted April 25, 2024
msg:I have been to Shenzhen more than a dozen times, mostly for business trips, and seldom walked around and felt the city. This time, in order to watch Lin Zhixuan's concert, I chose the Kempinski Hotel, which is close to the Spring Cocoon Stadium. After getting off the plane, I picked up the rented car. A BMW Series for two days was only less than 300 yuan, a conscience price. I navigated about 20 kilometers and went straight to the hotel to check in. The front desk handled the procedures very quickly and added two breakfasts very considerately. The hotel facilities are indeed a bit old, but fortunately they are well maintained and have all the basic functions. The room is not big. Although it is close to the downtown area, it is very quiet. The bedding is okay, but there is a socket on the side of the bed, which makes it a bit troublesome to charge the mobile phone. If you need to contact the housekeeping center, the response is very fast. The breakfast is standard, the variety is okay, but of course the flavor is not to be mentioned. The main advantage is the location. It is more than 10 minutes' walk from the Spring Cocoon Stadium, and you can walk there for the evening concert, especially after the show. Looking at the pedestrians and cars on the street, I was glad to have chosen Kempinski. There are many shopping malls and delicious food around. At 2 o'clock in the afternoon, I first chose Hanzhou on Dianping.com, a porridge shop nearby, and ordered shrimp porridge, chicken and matsutake porridge, and Chaozhou-style three-in-one. I regretted that the porridge was too large. One bowl was enough for two people. The taste was also unique in the capital. It was fragrant. The three-in-one was also unique. But after eating, I wondered what to do for dinner, because I had my eyes on the well-received Deyi Zhe, a Shunde dish, which I must try. I walked around Coast City casually. There was not much to see in the mall. There were mainly many delicious foods. I just regretted that I had little time and could not satisfy my appetite. Around five o'clock, the first wave arrived at Deyizhe. There were not many people yet. We ordered Shunde boneless three-flavor fish, raw Shuidong kale, and Shunde double-skin milk. The fish was so tender. There was a small three-jin haiwan (said to be a freshwater fish). There were three flavors: original, chopped pepper, and black bean sauce. Personally, I feel that the original flavor best reflects the original freshness of the fish. The blind spot raw kale is fresh and slightly bitter, light and refreshing. I have eaten double-skin milk in Shunde a long time ago. It is usually made from buffalo milk, tender and smooth like fat, with a full mouthful of milk. My wife praised it highly. When I returned to Beijing, I always regretted eating two bowls. The manager was very considerate. He introduced the origin of the three-flavor fish and also gave away kudzu, bamboo sugarcane, and water chestnut water. This meal was extremely satisfying. After watching the concert, I returned to the hotel near midnight and thought about having a midnight snack. I searched for Feiha Grilled Skewers, which is said to be the best in Nanshan. It is a few hundred meters away from the hotel. I lined up online and waited for half an hour on site. Finally, we ate it. Although it was very popular, we felt that it was a failure. The quality, taste and grilled smell of the skewers were very average. It seems that the locals‚Äô understanding of Northeastern grilled skewers is still very different. I really don‚Äôt recommend it! The next morning, I went from the hotel to Shenzhen Talent Park and ran for ten kilometers in the morning. The trail was very friendly. There were many people doing morning exercises. The environment was excellent. Across the sea, Hong Kong was vaguely visible. I checked out of the hotel in the morning and went straight to Dameisha Outlets to stroll around. In the afternoon, I drove to Dafen Oil Painting Village, the first in China, to visit Dafen Art Museum, to see the people who DIY oil paintings, and to feel the ocean painted in the village. It was worth the trip. I flew back to the capital at night. In short, this trip was originally expected to be unoriginal, but I booked Kempinski, and everything was fine. Music, food, shopping and painting, it was a very interesting trip to Shenzhen.

posted:Posted March 23, 2024
msg:I wanted to stay in a hotel for my wedding anniversary because I could relax and swim. I searched a lot of hotels, but some of them were relatively remote or did not have a heated swimming pool. Finally, I chose Shenzhen Hebinski Hotel.

Likes: It allows us to check in early and check out late at the hotel until 6pm. There are many restaurants near the hotel and the location is right next to Coast City. It is very convenient. This time we mainly bought a package that includes buffet breakfast and dinner buffet. The buffet seafood dinner is very rich. Although the appearance of the hotel is not very new, the feeling after checking in is okay. It can be seen that this hotel used to be very high-end. The front desk staff are very polite. This is really appreciated.

Areas that need improvement: We checked in on a Saturday, so the staff should be slow to close the dishes during breakfast on Sunday. Basically, they have to inform first comers every time that the dishes will be closed. F&B should improve the training of the staff when facing guests. There is no need to smile or feel a bit disinclined to work. This is not a complaint, I just want the hotel to do better so as not to waste the other advantages of the hotel.

The overall experience is not limited to the geographical advantage. There are all kinds of restaurants.
